class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1961px;">     <h2 id="section1502957143419" device-type="phone,tablet,wearable">healthStore.deleteData<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>deleteData(request: SamplePointDeleteRequest | SamplePointDeleteRequest[]): Promise&lt;void&gt;</p>     <p>删除数据采样点，使用Promise异步方式。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong>SystemCapability.Health.HealthStore</p>     <p><strong>设备行为差异：</strong>该接口在Phone、Tablet中可正常调用，在Wearable中返回1002700001错误码。</p>     <p><strong>起始版本：</strong>5.0.0(12)</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.52.8.1.5.1.1"         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.52.8.1.5.1.3" width="6.02%">          <p>必填</p></th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.52.8.1.5.1.4" width="48.6%">          <p><strong>说明</strong></p></th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="19.45%">          <p>request</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25.929999999999996%">          <p><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/health-api-healthstore#section1680218365918">SamplePointDeleteRequest</a> | <a         <td class="cellrowborder" width="48.6%">          <p>删除数据采样点请求。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p class="msonormal"><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.52.10.1.3.1.1" width="32.16%">          <p>类型</p></th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.52.10.1.3.1.2" width="67.84%">          <p>说明</p></th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="32.16%">          <p>Promise&lt;void&gt;</p></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="67.84%">          <p>无结果返回的Promise对象。</p></td>        </tr>
